present cronycle hystory rome written batayle whiche romayns iugurth vsurper kyngdome numydy lande numydy parte countrey affryke whiche raygned somtyme kynge named massinissa felowe frende empyre rhome massinissa thre sonnes thus named micipsa manastabal galussa deth manastabal galussa first brother named micipsa obtayned kyngdome numydy alone without partyner custome numydy heritage wont deuided among brethern equal porcions dyscease theyr parentes whome suche heritage issueth micipsa crowned kynge hole numydy two sonnes first called adherbal seconde hiempsall brother manastabal whiche departed left behynde hym one bastarde sonne named iugurth grandfather massinissa bequethed none heritage left hym priuate without lande lyuelodde asmoche vnlaufully borne kynge micipsa moued pyte compassyon agaynst iugurth cosideryng brother sonne without conforte receyued hym house cherisshed hym thynges dyde owne sonnes iugurth grewe stature grewe gyftes belongynge nature became right strong hardy knyght also excellent wysdome courage myght moche elder two sonnes micispa named adher ball hiempsall tyme micipsa cosydered ouryng age manlynes wysdome iugurth parte whan remebred feble yongth vnexpert owne two sonnes aduisemet mynde sore troubled wt drede est dethe iugurth myght inuade vsurpe vnto hymselfe kyngdome numydy owne two sonnes beyng nat power defende theselfe micipsa thynges cosydred determined obiect iugurth vnto paryll warre meanes assay might fortune hym slayne batell therfore tyme ye romains hauyng scipio capitaine beseged cyte numance micipsa sent vnto romains ye batayle great socours horsmen fotemen made iugurthe captayn ouer dyde trustynge possible lykely ynough iugurth knyght yonge lusty desirous honour myght chauce fortune slayne batayle sayd conclusion fortuned moche contrary boldnesse strength iugurthe warre well proued knowen many noble valiant actes chyualry dyd wherby wanne moche laude glory great loue fauour nat onely scipio captaine also noblest men romayne army insomoche warre fynisshed cyte numance distroyed captaine scipio assembled hole army magnificent fauorable wordes comended iugurth merueylous laudes done rewarded hym many riche gyftes chyualry sent hym agayne kynge micipsa letter wherin also commended iugurth great laude praysyng instigacion whiche thynges befell kyng micipsa nat long desyred nothyng ye deth iugurth nowe coueted nought somoche conseruacion lyfe helth nat long adopted hym sonne ordayned testamet hym one heyres partiner kyngdome two naturall sonnes whiche ordinauce neuer chaunged departyng increased fauour benefites agaynst ye iugurth leauynge hym nat onely partiner kyngdome also treasours besyde decryed hym protectour two naturall sonnes theyr porcions kyngdome sone ordinauce kyng micipsa departed fro lyfe whan ye thre prince adherball hiempsall iugurth determined amonge tyme whan treasoure shulde deuided boundes kyngdome lymited eche one parte assemble grewe dissencion betwene hiempsall iugurth occasyon wherof iugurth shortely slewe hiempsall treason gyle hiempsall slayne iugurthe fixed mynde possesse hole kyngdome numidy wherfore prepared great strong army agaynst brother adherball last whan bothe mette batayle army adherball ouerthrowen hymselfe put flyght adherball thus ouercome spoyled kyngdome fledd vnto rome senatours declared tyrannous cruelte iugurth agaynst hym comitted agaynst brother hiempsall cruelly murdred desiryng socours senatours wt pytefull wordes lamentable complayntes conclusion decreed senatours x noble men rome shulde sent embassadours numydy departed affr ke towarde rome iugurth sette mynde yet one agayn inuade vsurpe part ye kyngdome belonged ad herball assignemet embassadours wherfore assembled newe army inuaded kyngdome adherball theyr tentes moneth ianuary coldest sharpest season wynter dyde bycause trusted ende batayle tyme therby wynne thanke worshyppe el thentet gete money iugurh grautyng vnto hym peace rest tyme costrayne aulus drede aulus vnderstadyng persued folowed hym egarly hastely without aduisment ord r uision whan iugurth sawe attised drawen romains place fyght auauntage anone assayled embatayled fyersly batayle ouercame romains putte flyght next morne iugurth aulus came togyder communicacion last trewes stryken bytwene bothe party maner co dicions romains shuld passe vnder spere signe subieccion ouercome without hurt afterwarde within ten dayes shulde depart numidy done whan tydyng herof brought rome citie troubled drede displeasure shamefull trewes aulus disconfiture flyght romayne army adnulled none effecte season sayde wyt age syckenesse feble dull small valoure therfore suche thynges space enacted done without wysdome reason whanne hiempsall herde iugurth thus speke answered sayenge pleased hym ryght well shulde done within thre yeres sayd father micipsa hath adopted sonne testamet ordayned partiner kyngdome whiche worst vnaduised dede euer dyd yonge olde wherfore iugurth accordynge owne ordynaunce must fyrst adnulled broken whiche done brother shall nat greatly contende remenant wordes hiempsall pearsed hert iugurth profoudely thanne man thought suspected wherfore tyme forwarde wrathe wordes drede losse porcyon kyngdome mynde great trouble anguysshe somoche then forthe went aboute ymagyned ordayned onely reuoulued mynde gyle treason hiempsall myght caught daunger whanne purpose proceded slowly forwarde consydrynge frowarde desyre vnrefrenable appeti e mynde coude nat mytigated pacyfied concluded bryng enterprise effect maner meanes outher preuy treason anone prepared secretly great company armed men whome commaunded bringe vnto hym heed hiempsall trenched body executynge dede commaunded ruled numydyan whiche counterfayted key done sayd numydyan slepynge theyr beddys suspectynge suche treason wakened dynne stert vp mette theyr ennemyes defendynge themselfe vayne leyser arme themselfe therfore slayne anone vnarmed men armed apointed myschefe whan treatours longe sought hiempsall myght nat fynde hym serched nerely euery hyd corner secret close place brast open full dynne mengled noyse clamour moche sought nerely last foude hiempsall hyd open warre bytwene adherball aduised hymselfe well remembraunce first batayle iugurth nat able contende hym batayle force armes ouer cofidence trust frendshyp romayns inconstat numidyans leaned ennemy myght haue moued coragious hert neuerthelesse adherball determined mynde suffre thynges take many iniuries paciently rather agayn begyn batayle iugurth sayd batayle foughten bytwene bothe dishonour also great dammage suffrance adherball mynde iugurth nat pacified lessed cruelte pacience adherball abated nat ire iugurth augmeted redy cocluded mynde inuade ye hole kyngdoe numidy therfore began agayn newe nat copany reuers myghty great army assembled togyder demeanyng open warre chalangyng openly hole empire numidy power proceded land adherball wastyng townes fyld euery syde dryuing away prayes catell rich increasyng corage men drede ennemis whan adherball sawe come point must nedes abandon gyue ouer kyngdome el mayntayne force armes constrayned extreme necessite assembled empareyled army aswell myght thesame proceded forth mete iugurth last two hoostes adherball iugurth approched rested nere togyder besyde towne named cirtha nat ferre distant seecoost asmoch day drewe nere nyght vtterly intollerable authorite senate betrayed cruell fiers ennemy iugurth empire falsly betrayed mennes handes possession comen wele hath ben put sale iugurth ye senator bothe home cite also army calphurnius cosull insomoch examinacion nat made herof nat punysshed culpable fautie herin thyng shall remayne vnto v must passe lyfe vnder obedience bondage thus haue done v shall kepe subiection yf nat thus exhorte coueyt rather citezins shulde yll well speke thintet ye shulde nat fauour forbere fewe iniust yll disposed men vtter distruction good men shuld procede suche indiscrete fauour also cursed moreouer mysdoers punysshed last theyr nombre shalbe abated decresed fewe vniust men lesse wrong done whome wronge done nedeth nat call socour helpe thus better leaue good dede vnrewarded yll rome pthe xxi chap whyle thynges hand done rome meane tyme chefe ye soudyours whiche calphurnius lefte behynd hym numidy folowed maners behauour theyr captayne dyde many vngoodly myscheuous dedes corrupt golde delyuerd agayne iugurth olyphantes gyuen calphurnius tyme ye peace graunted true first taken bytwene solde iugurth traytours whiche fledde hym vnto romayns army spoyled robbed people numidy whiche redy peace romayns yelded themselfe great shamefull violence couetyse infected theyr mynd ben vniuersall contagion pest ence nowe wyll returne mater left concernynge cassius iudge vyage numidy bryng iugurth vnto rome phowe iugurth came rome cassius howe behaued hymselfe xxii chapyter cayus memmius name comens gaue comaundemet cassius accordynge ordinaunce inacted spede hym toward numidy bydde iugurth come rome vnder suerte co dicion rehersed whan estate whiche knewe theselfe culpable vnderstode maruelusly abassed wham cassius come iugurth nat withstandyng ereful part confidence cause asmoche knewe hymselfe fauty owne conscience yet cassius aduysed hym induced hym bycause yelded hymselfe come vnto rome without wolde rather proue romayns strength violence theyr mercy pyte moreouer sayd cassius promised also owne fayth trouth wolde come rome answere truly suche thynges shulde demaunded hym shulde safely go come without impediment cassius good name tyme iugurth asmoche cofidence fayth promes alone promes assurance hole cite last iugurth cosented go rome cassius wherfore enduce romayns pyte arayed hymselfe rude aparell agaynst honour royall moche vyle myserable cassius came rome nat kyng poorly small co pany nat withstandyng mynde moche confermed assured bolded confort whiche corrupted rewardes vnder whose defence supportacion comytted moche cruelty yet behaued hym gyftes newe assone come rome great reward induced lorde rome named caius bebius one tectours comenty supporter mayntener cause among mo whose dishonest vnmesurable couetise trusted assuredly defended agaynst lawe punysshmentes due vnto demerites comenty rome violently sore wrathe agaynst iugurth comaunded haue hym prison kepe hym bandes wolde acordyng lawe punysshment dethe shulde taken hym theyr mortall ennemy wold nat shortly cofesse discouer felowes partiners supporter cruell dedes caius memius heryng herof called togyder comenty alayed mocyon wrath theyr myndes apeasyng theyr vnauysed rancour requirynge kepe fayth trouth cite promysed iugurthe clere inuiolate vndefyled thus dyd memmius exhort regarded set conseruacion dignite rome parfourmynge satisfyeng wrath ire rude co men whan sylence made among assemble anone iugurth brought forth memmi began speke hym demurely rehersyng openly recountyng corrupt estate rome treasure cruelly agaynst ryght done many abhomynable dedes rome also numidy agaynst kyng micipsa sonnes slayne adherball hiempsall falsly dysceyued kyng micipsa wasted ye kyngdome numidy howebeit sayd memmius romayns knewe well supporter yet wold iugurth shulde openly discouer accuse hymselfe wherfore desyred hym truely cofesse name whose supportacion bolde comyt many imoderate cruell dedes sayng wold cofesse disclose trouth myght haue great trust confydence ye fauour clemece mercy people rome wold nat shulde profet sylence noble men rome supported also shulde dystruction vndoyng hymselfe ryches also poynt memmi ceassed wordes helde hym styll anone iugurth comauded commente make answere whan reddy haue spoken caius bebius whome corrupted treasour haue made mencion commauded hym hold pea somoche howebeit people sore moued displeasure put hym feare exclamacion agaynst hym angry countenance often violently rennynge vpon hym token yre dyspleasure neuerthelesse frowarde counsell bebius ouercame theyr thretnyng insomoche iugurth wolde nothyng speke dysclose thus people derision abused departed cogregacion assemble myndes iugurthe calphurnius theyr partyners inhansed increased boldnesse whiche troubled moche ferefull whan iugurth first sende brought examined phow iugurth encreased crueltie rome renued murdre sleayng noble man stocke micipsa occasion wherof constrayned departe rome batayle renewed agayne whan towne cirtha yelded adherball slayne whefore trusted nat iugurth saue hymselfe fled numidy vnto rome nowe lorde rome named albinus whiche creat consull partyng felowe named minucius next yere fautie tyll tyme vnderstode sawe enuy displeasure taken agaynst dede passed fauoure rewardes whiche gyuen rome yt last gyftes foude socoures ayde howebeit first accion accusemet layed agaynst hym hym commaunded senatours depart italy ennemy romayns theyr empyre whan departed lytell without rome sayde loked often backewarde behynde hym spekyng secretly hymselfe last spake playnly audience suthull whiche towne treasours iugurth layed towne walles water moutaygnes nature strongly defended without walles buylded heyght mountaygne broken forefronte great playne fenne marrayse grounde resysted theyr ennemies valyantly fully assured prefyxed dye lyke men yf fortune shulde graunt none meanes escape instant danger cowardes hydde themselfe caues secrete place yf myght fynde boldest vsed suche chaunces conforted theyr felowes whiche ferefull vnexpert suche chaunces warre howbeit none bolde well assured hymselfe bothe great drede danger maruayle euery place sydes inuironed authorite maners wherfore metellus newe capytayne hadde moche thought besynesse suche corrupt vicious maners company farre order hadde helpe good hope confort multitude thus howe beit sawe tyme election newe cosuls drawe nere yf also vnderstode romayns dayly loked ende warre cause nat withstandyng yet cocluded nat begyn warre tyll excercysed vsed soudyors besynesse labour aft instruction custome olde captayns vsed tyme albinus astonyed aduersite myschaunce brother aulus murdre hoost purposed nat depart romayns prouince whiche affrike kept soudyors alway ydell theyr tentes longe somer season lasted long authorite somoche chaunged place except corrupt sauoure place el necessite vitayle costrayned remoue accordyng custome maner warryours amonge watche euery man came went owne pleasure absented theselfe theyr standardes whan lyked scolyons page wandred day nyght mengled among horseman chiefe soudyours without order many rouers dyspersed abrode destroyed countrey fyghtynge agaynst small village nat agaynst citees townes caryed away sayd village prayes catell inhabitates ledde away also prisoner prayes stryuyng togyder myght haue chaunged sayde roberies marchauntes delycious strong wynes caryed strange countreis better wyne grewe coutrey suche delycious thyng solde away vitayles delyuered theyr capytayns among comen dayly bought theyr bread finally euer shame rebuke longyng couetyse lechery coude outher sayd done ymagined man vsed hoost among shamefull dedes ought named metellus hehaued hym selfe myghty wyse man nat lesse difficultie hardnesse ben batayle foughte agaynst enne mies myddes great couetyse voluptuesite cruelty syngulerly indued teperaunce merueylous good maner vsed coartynge fautes wherfore first begynnynge withdrewe auoyded army commaundemet ordinaunce occasyons styred soudyours suche slouth cowardyse voluptuosite commaunded vnder great payne person shulde hardy sell among soudyours nouther bread vitayle reddy dressed saue co men uisyon page waterlaggers scolyons shuld nat coe nere army folowe none comen simple sodyours shulde kepe mentayne seruaunt beest theyr tentes vyage whyle moued fro place place inconuenyences first redressed refourmed amended fautes mesured wysdome craft policy refourmynge lytell lytell done haue soudyours occupyed moued dayly place place nat wayes comen vsed harde vnoccupyed wayes caused dayly cast dychesse trench army intent shuld nat waxe slouthfull vicious ouermoch rest ydlenesse ordayned often watche among euery nyght hymselfe acompanyed vnder captayns heed officer often serched yf watch truely kept copassyng army euery syde whyle remoued chaunged place somtyme forwarde amonge first somtyme rerewarde hynder part anone myddes ouerseynge theyr order intent none shulde passe order graunt hym owne lyfe lyfe chyldren onely concernyng thyng wolde yelde handes romayns metellus knewe well ynough long tyme often experience profe yt numidian naturall disposicion vnfaythfull mouable vnstable myndes newfangled moche desyrous newe besynesse newelties wherfore began embassadours iugurth tastyng prouyng mynde eche lytell lytell separatly one one whan knewe somwhat inclined purpose promysed great gyftes promocion wold pleasure hym senatours people rome last counsayled desyred delyuer iugurth hym alyue specially myght brought yf coude nat delyuer hym outher quicke deed whan made apoyntement secretly thembassadours deuyded sonder one one openly euery man myght shewed togyder thynges pleasure shuld certyfie kynge iugurth concernynge embassade within fewe dayes whan sawe hoost moost redy contrary iugurth remoued tentes addressed hym army redy aray went forward numidy contrary similitude warre vyllages cotages full men feldes full beest tylmen euery moche plenty people yonge olde namely rude people tyllers grounde whiche styll fled army foretyme feare last whan sawe defence socoure kynges lewtenantes left townes village lodge went forthe mete metellus withall humilite proceded forwarde togyder army aray redy armoure defended theyr ennemies ben nere hande serchynge countrey abrode euery syde espyes doutynge treason thynkyng token subiection face cloke couer treason nat well knowe whether douted greuous peace ware whyle absent present pnat farre way whiche metellus helde army towne numidyans moche acustomed frequented marchantes italy strange countreis princypall thyder thinkynge case required concours marchantes resortyng thyder good prouision vytayls shulde great defence conseruacyon hym army bothe warre peace whan citezins sawe purueyance made vitels instautly done mekely besechyng requyring hym peace yeldyng vnto hym euery thynge onely reserued owne lyfe lyfe chyldren metellus sende embassadours home agayne attysed prodycion maister iugurth done agayn take socour hyll shuld prohibyted dryuen bacwarde agayne handes iugurth done sodenly dyd trupetes blowen anone withall inuaded set vpon company metellus euery syde numidyens assayled bete downe stryke ennemies agayne ioyne wt iugurth taught numidiens horsbake batayle whan shulde begyn assayle romayns shulde nat kepe themselfe togyder nere asmoche dyspersed coude diuers place one company soudyours iugurth coude nat auoyed repell romayns whiche assayled bycause mo nombre thefore compassed trapped behynde sydes betyn dysioyned company fortuned fle numidyans auantage romayns fled feldes assayled romayns backe halfe el bothe sydes dyuers companyes sawe auayle expediet fle agayne hyll set first ordynaunce also auantage therby horse acustomed mountaynes combred wayes wherfore mounted lesse difficultie cotrary wyse romayns sharpnes hylles lacke vse coude nat folowe assedyng without moch difficulte payne paryll nat withstandynge iugurth men auantage countrey grounde yet batayle sydes variable vncertayne vngoodly myserable beholde best men sonest slayne moost ieopardy courage valyant myndes bolde hertes romayns worth gyle treason iugurthyns bothe sydes boldest moost auauced hymself sonest ouerthrowen deuyded owne company hand ennemies gaue place yelded themselfe agayne folowed chased ennemies fleyng myght make theirty good resysted eyther partie manly none party kept vnder standerdes folowed nat order batayle kept none order array euery man resysted defended hymself ther moost ieopardy paryll layed hym endeuoyred hymselfe withstande vyolence ennemis hye valyantise armour defensyfs dartes horse romayns numidyans soudyours page confounded mengledde togyder without orde ordynaunce obserued nothyng done dyscression soudyours counsell captayns vnauysed fortune chaunce gouerned bysynesse day vnstable batayle committed rule fortune thus passed forth moche day great murder slaughter yet styll ende batayle vncertayne none knewe whytherpartye shulde haue vyctorye last bothe party labour heat began languysshe become wery metellus vnderstandynge numidyans lesse resysted infyghtyng dyde assembled gathered togyder agayne soudyours lytell lytell without tary restored aray set agayne order iiii cohortes taken forth legyons set agaynst fotemen ennemies metellus thus assembled company great parte oppressed woundes werynesse withdrewe self hyll named hyer place batayle refresshe rest themselfe whan metellus sayd reasembled agayne began infewe wordes pray exhort suche maner po worthy trusty soudyours companyons dyscourage nat selfe batayle lette nat olde noblenesse nowe fayle suffre nat ennemies wont put trust flyght nowe ouercome ferefull myndes remebre well ye dysposed cowardly fle ye haue tentes cyties townes castels maner place defece wherto ye may renne refuge saue selfe helth hope defence onely armoure strength specially bolde hert wherfore dere frendes remebre olde worshyp suffre nat hole empire rome suffre dysworshyp temerous themselfe foure elyphantes taken remenat fourty nombre slayne whan done co pany rutilius nat withstandynge fatigate weryed great iourneis also moche labour orderyng tentes sayd batayle skirmysshe neuertheles whan sawe metellus chefe captayne taryed longer thought wold haue done yf thynge happened well hym ordred themselfe redy diligently went backwarde agayne mete hym falshode gyle iugurth numidyans caused besy diliget circumspect euery thyng sauegard lyues suffred nothyng slouly delayeng whan iourney darknesse nyght companyes party nat fare sondre one bothe party approched togyder nat knowyng eche ben ennemies one agaynst making noyse clamour eche one increasyng fear warryours ar wont begynnyng batayle insomoch miserable dystruction murdre almost ben comitted bytwene imprudet negligence espyes horsmen whiche sent bytwene bothe sydes nat diligece wyselyer espied treuth mater whan party knewe eche sadnes feare tourned great ioye gladnesse soudyours ioyfully anone met togyder one salutyng welcomyg one shewed actes done bothe party ioyous bothe sydes euery man commendyng exaltyng owne dedes also ded vnto heuen myrthe gladnesse aswell worthy men vnworthy cowardys ascrybed themselfe worthynesse certes busynesse often happeneth syde hath victorie suche cowardes rude vncrafty exalteth enioyeth may bost themselfe mennes dedes worthynesse cotrary wyse partie ouercom though many good warryours noble worthy men yet ar reputed coward without policy bycause mennes cowardyse aduersyte fortune thus fareth skirmysshes batayle whan metellus rutilius haue sayd mette togyder suche wordes po worthy soudyours ye se nowe hardest labour ouerpassed boldnesse manhode wherfore exhort ye lyke courage resydue besynesse whiche shalbe lyght easy comparyson ouerpassed begynnyng first pwhat wast dystruction metellus made lande numidy first batayle flyght iugurth gyle iugurth agaynst metellus pthe xxxiii chapter wha metellus vnderstode espyes mynde iugurth cotinued yet styll olde coude coueniently cotende hym dyfficultie therof metellus thus knowyng aduised hymselfe many thynges namely consydred nat different egall bothe party executyng therof yf vpper hand ouer iugurth put hym flyght yet lost mo men damage ouercomyng hym iugurth whiche ouercome consyderacion metellus purposed contende hym playne feldes ordered batayle maner execute warre hym thensforthe determyned metellus hole hoost ordynaunce went forth moost ryche plentyfull place numidy wasted dystroyed feldes coutrey euery syde toke without resystence castels townes nat strongly defended walles dychesse garnyson brent bete downe grounde suche came way able bere harnesse full growen age apt batayle slewe ryd hande thynkynge mo slewe fewer aduersaries ennemies shulde haue contende agaynst hym comaunded soudyors spare robbery prayes gaue althyng hauocke among soudyours pfor feare crueltie many numidyens yelded themselfe romayns gaue vnto hostage vytayls sodyours thynges necessary abundatly insome townes whiche taken metellus sette defence garnyson nede requyred fortified sufficiently besynesse troubled mynd iugurth moche batayle foughten great dammage disconfort men lost people way meane thus reioyced greatly comended metellus namely caused iugurth put trust helth onely fleyng moutayns wyldernesse whiche magnificent proude fear cowardyse aulus predecessour metellus wherfore fortunat glorious dedes metellus senatours decreed comauded ouer cite sacrifice suffrage done ydolles citezyns whiche ferefull sore troubled doutyng vnsure chauce incertayne fortue ende warre demened nowe meanes wayes might honour cofusion iugurth neuertheles well ware puttyng hymselfe danger ennemies ware exchuynge oportunite gyle euery place went remebred well cosydred often laude glorie foloweth metellus whan iugurth herof certified hasted hym gret iourneis ouerpassed copany metellus came towne zamam hym exhorted inhabitantes boldly defende walles farthermore assigned socour helpe suche fled romayns brought hym tidyng treatours surest men whiche iugurth coude nat dysceyue hym wolde yelde agayne romayns whome forsaken betrayed thyng nat sure whan iugurth ioyned soudyours garnison socours towne castell ordred apoynted thynges acordynge mynde promysed agayne hole army tyme nede done departed towne preuy secret place knewe countrey therby whan metellus iourney towarde zaman sende marius prouision whete corne vitayle army vnto towne named sicca whiche first towne forsoke iugurth yelded marius batayle late foughten iugurth great damage whan iugurth knowledge herof went thyder nyght priuely elect soudyors whan marius sped mater redy departe forth towne iugurth redy gate assayle romayns cruelly cryeng hye voyce towne exhortynge assayle romayns also backe halfe saynge fortune offred chaunce noble act excellent glorious dede yf wolde folowe desyre shulde restore hym agayne kyngdome themselfe libertie thensforth passe tyme without peryll without danger drede certaynely marius nat boldely strongly broken towne standerdes men armes thickest ennemies whiche gate towne part wolde haue broken theyr oth promesse whiche made metellus whan first yelded themselfe cite hym myndes numidiens vnstedfast mouable iugurth conforted soudyours resysted romayns lytell season wha marius company began encrease violence agaynst iugurthyns fiersely prease vpon anone slayne resydue fled maister iugurth daunger ouerpassed marius departed then towarde towne zaman last came thyder safe copany besynesse sped wherfore sent pthis samam towne bylded playne groude without hylles water nere defended rather ye warke mannes hande nature place fayled nothyng necessary batayle well garnissed men ordynaunce vitayls armour anone whan marius come metellus acordynge tyme place made redy thynges necessary compassed walles euery syde wt army assignynge euery one vndercapitayns separate place towne assayle deuoyre shewe manhode whan euery thynge thus ordred metellus commaunded sounde assaut trumpettes cla yons romayns immediatly assayled towne euery syde wt horryble noyse clamoure numidiens therof nat drad abode styll kept selfe sylence nat ben displeased prouoked batayle howebeit kept walles euery man part hym assigned redy resyst assayle romayns anone batayle begone romayns exercysed occupyed themselfe euery man wt suche wepyn coud best handell expert slynges thrue plummettes thinhabitauntes towne garnyson resysted manly rowled downe ouertourned great weyghty stone suche nerest vndermyned walles pytched downe vpon dartes iauelyns pykes firebrandes also great brennynge polles faggottes blockys ouercouered pytche brestone ardenly flamyng boldly ouertourned scalyng ladder slewe ouerthrue suche scaled walles whiche farther towne prease coude nat approche nere walles cast themselfe thus toke intentife hede batayle forgate themselfe semed ben felowes batayle whan marius besyged towne syde vnderstode maner behauour inhabitautes garyson abated fiersnes policy slowe besyegyng towne fayning trust cofidence wynne suffred numidyens within towne beholde batayle kynge whyle without resystence besynesse wha sawe intentifely beholdyng batayle amased besynesse felowes also hym euery thing nat coueyted desyred euery man became hym well reason cotented pleased satisfied honour whiche owne nat desyre thyng vnmete degre finally exhorted couselled hym beware desyre yt thing romayns laufully might denyed vnto hym cosydring hauyng regarde lynage auncet pafter metellus couselled marius wordes lyke coude nat tourne apease mynde answered hym last assone coude couenietly foly partes feryng lest nacion anone shuld assayle ouercomers ouercome whan wasted weryed batayls brought extremite wherfore cosydred toke truys bytwene bothe auoyed long variance bytwene made agremet couenant messangers embassadours bothe party shulde depart city one certayne day houre assigned place messangers city shulde mete togyder shulde euer taken boundes march coutrey nacions city without contencion variance bryng apoyntmet effect conclusyon forth cite cyren chosen two part sende forth day houre apoynted lykewyse carthage send two breterne eche named phylene swyftly sped iourney cyreneses went moch slowly whether fortuned negligece chauche knowe lytell trueth knowen certayne coostes tempeste wynde weder wont let men long iourney lykewyse vpon see cause whan euyn place wyde bare wtout thing growynge wynde ryseth styreth small sande groude sande moued great violence wynd wont fyll face mouthes eyen passeth way dust sande thus often lettyng syght iournay longed hyndred whan cyrenenses sawe themselfe somwhat ouerflowe late iournay fered punysshement retournynge home negligece blamyng accused carthaginenses obiectyng sayeng come forth cite tyme assigned thus troubled mater brake ordynance shortly speke cirenenses cocluded rather suffre deth thynge possible retourne home agayn ouercoe wherfore carthaginenses desyred codicion apoyntment made indifferet equall bytwene party cireneses cosented therto put carthagineses choyse whyther wold quicke buryed place whiche desyred march boudes el cirenenses vnder codicion shulde cede forwarde place whiche desyred march quicke buryed vnder maner ii bretherne named phylene alowed graunted codicion subduyng abandonyng bodyes deth profet wele contrey cite carthage buryed quicke wherfore carthaginenses place buryed raysed halowed ii auters worshyp remebrance two brethern set encrese contrey owne lyues auters preset day called phylene auts name ii brethern named phylenis therunder buryed sayd wele contrey also besyde memorial wtin cite carthage many thing ordayned ye gret honour remembrance worthy dede pbut nowe wyll leaue mater reteurne purpose phow iugurth assembled newe army rude getulyans agaynst romayns associated vnto hym bocchus kynge mauriens strengthe hym batayle agaynst metellus pthe xlvii chapyter whan iugurth lost citie thala one strongest city lande sayd consydred well kyngdome place stronge ynough resyst myght metellus wherfore hasted hym small copany desertes great wyldernesse fleyng owne contrey last came lande getulians whiche maner people rude wylde without order maners season nought knowyng preemynet honour fame romayne empire people iugurth assembled multitude togyder lytell lytell enduced taught custome exercyse folowe order chyualry kepe array insue standerdes obey comaundementes capitayns discerne haue knowlege signifiaunce soundes trumpettes obserue poyntes belongyng warfare chyualry thyng otherlike necessary batayle iugurth ceassed nat prepare ordayne diligence pmoreouer prouoked vnto fauour felowshyp great rewardes moch gretter promise suche nere frendes bocchus kyng mauries whose helpe hymselfe went kyng bocchus moche desyred hym quarell hym warre agaynst romayns request iugurth bocchus agreed somoch asmoche first begynnynge warre bocchus sent vnto rome embassadours desyre romayns amyte bonde cotinuall peace bytwene hym nat withstandyng peticion peace moche expediet necessary romayns diuerse cosideracions namely bycause warre nat lesse nat grauted meane fewe rome blynded wt auarice wont sell money euery thyng honest dishonest also befor tyme doughter iugurth spoused sayed bocchus bonde frendshyp affinite among numidies mauriens reputed effect bycause ar wont euery man haue diuerse many wyues acordyng substace richesse x mo ar abylite power metayne kyng bycause ar power substace therfore haue mo thus mynde fauour distract diuersly deuyded wyues multitude bycause haue many reserue none speciall bed felowe wherfore ar reputed vyle lytell set one maner thus affinite bytwene two kyng iugurth bocchus lytell set small thyng auayled besynesse nat withstandynge hoostes cae togyder place apoynted therto gyuen taken fayth trueth one fidelite obserued bytwene iugurth greatly inhauced lyfted vp mynde bocchus wordes sayeng romains iniust grounded auarice without suffisance measure comen ennemies euery man euery contrey asmoch quarell agaynst bocchus agaynst hym one selfe cause warre agaynst also agaynst many nacions whiche cause onely pleasure great lordshyp rich cause kyngdomes aduers cotrary hymselfe enmy cause nat longe tyme carthagineses aftwarde perses kyng macedony subdued vndone romayns without iust tytle cause batyle saue onely ambicion enuy whiche romayns agaynst tyme come euery nacyon whiche shulde haue welth richesse shuld become ennemies romayns inordynat pride saciable couetyse pwith wordes otherlyke iugurth moued mynde bocchus agaynst romayns somoche anone day apoynted bytwene bothe kynges procede forth togyder towne cyrtha assayle power conioyned towne purposed first besige bycause metellus left towne prayes prisoner taken iugurth also moche owne ordynauce left voyde impedyment voyage thus iugurth thought expedient myght wyn towne assaut rescous metellus thought shuld moost honour profet el yf romayne capitayne metellus army shulde come socours towne thought hymselfe bocchus shuld gyue batayle metellus iugurth craft subtylte hasted hereto somoche tangle bocchus warre place shulde moued bytwene hym romayns lest bocchus prologyng tyme myght rather encline peace warre leasour shuld haue taken better cou sell aduisement iugurth suspected begynnynge metellus processe tyme wolde desyre bocchus nat medyll warre assistyng part iugurth mentayning cause phowe metellus vsed hymselfe herynge two kynges confederat agaynst hym certifyed prouynce numidy assigned marius new consull c ssed warre none pthe xlviii chapyter whanne metellus knewe two kynges associate togyder thought nat fyght rasshely without prouisyon euery place aduantage nat wont often tymes first tyme ouercome iugurth within feldes well surely defended kept hymselfe abydinge commynge two kynges nat farre towne cirtha dyd thynking best know myght maners codicions mauriens first wold fight bycause newe ennemies therfore maners vnknowen hym whan sawe best auantage thought gyue batayle pin meane tyme whyle metellus taryed commyng two kynges letter brought vnto hym rome certifyed hym prouince numidy comytted gyuen marius newe consull herde longe tyme sayd marius elect cosull first tyme vnderstode prouince numidy comitted hym cause metellus moued displeased moch longed measure honesty somoch coud neyther refrayne eyen wepyng measure tong spekyng yll marius metellus synguler noble worthy man condicions displeasure mynde toke ouer womanly tenderly hert namely cause condicion reputed procede proude hert metellus thought meruayle though noble hert moued kyndled anger iniury wrong done hym many sayd metellus toke great sorowe displeasure bycause victorie almoost optayned shulde pulled handes selfe hauyng labour paryll man tryumphe honour playne mater indifferently write nat vnknowen wysest romayns dignite auauncement honour marius greued metellus moch dyd owne iniury wolde nat haue taken heuely prouince numidy taken hym ben gyuen noble men tha marius wherfore metellus let first besynesse sayd displeasure purposed nat vexe hymselfe thensforth thanke profet also thought foly take hande charge another mannes mater owne paryll labour payne wherfore send messangers kyng bocchus desyring hym nat become ennemy romayns without occasion sayeng yet suche case myght adioyne romayns felowshyp loue amyte shulde moche better hym profitable batayle howbeit trusted gretly power richesse treasour yet ought nat change certayne thynges thynges incertayne euery batayle begyn easy lyght ver harde thynge ende whan one begon begynning endynge therof nat alway power one man warre may begon coward wretch nat left agayne ceassed whan pleaseth hym strongest maister hauynge vpper hande finally hym better prouide hymselfe kyngdome began nat adioyne myngle goodes treasour fortune estate royall florisshyng goodes fortune iugurth lost distroyed vttermost embassadours metellus came kyng bocchus shewed hym capitayns wyll sayd vnder suche sentence whiche wordes metellus bocchus answered agayne benignely mekely ynough sayng desyred nothyng peace saue pyte compassion aduers miserable fortune iugurth iugurth myght suffred also haue frendshyp amyte romayns forgyuenesse sayd bocchus wolde gladly agre euery thynge desyred metellus euery thyng shuld accorded bytwene capitayne metellus heryng answere bocchus agayne sent messangers hym replyeng agaynst requestes sayenge peticions agaynst iustice reason also metellus embassadours desyred many thyng bocchus whome bocchus graunted alowed denyed maner tyme ouerpassed proceded forth massangers often goyng comynge bytwene bothe suche maner warre batayle remayned vntouched depended nat medled metellus dyd greatly coueyt desyre mynde bycause wolde kepe sure laude wonne also owne paryll dammage wolde nat auantage auance marius thynge whiche hym belonged pbut wyll leaue speke metellus retourne speke marius whiche contrary wyll noble men rome creat consull fauour comens lykewyse haue writen pof great ordynauce preparacyon whiche marius newe cosull made agaynst iugurth warre numidy pthe xlix chapyter bvt marius haue sayde elect consull great desyre instauce comen people whiche also comytted hym prouince numidy marius seyng hymselfe thus auanced euer agaynst noble men rome nowe specially fiers mynde stately besy displease hurt state tyme one one whyle altogyder often tymes boosted sayd goten consulshyp maugre wyll pray spoyling goten ennemies men ouercome many boostynge wordes spake owne commendacion great displeasure anger vnto estate rome meane tyme forgat nat prepare euery thyng necessary warre wherof charge rested hym execute agaynst iugurth thensforth demauded senatours comens newe supplement soudyours repare restore army numidy metellus many slayne many deed sickenesse thus army sore deminisshed called also socors suche nacions marched thempire kyng whiche cofederate conioyned felowshyp romayns moreouer raysed vp italy nere rome many strongest bolde mennes bodyes namely hymselfe proued warre suche warfare proued dedes nat suche boosted fame namely olde soudyours longe haunted warre pardoned therof power man costrayn warre without owne fre assent bycause cotinued styll warre season assigned captayns treated marius fayre flateryng paynted wordes redy go hym warfare beit senatours contrary hym yet durst nothyng deny vnto hym belongyng besynesse gladly good wyll decreed shulde rayse chuse soudyours fulfyll nombre wer lost batayle contrey numidy dyd gret loue marius thought shuld lese outher execucion batayle intended iugurth el fauour people wold refuse go forth warre marius costrayned olde loue myght tourne newe malyce hatered agaynst hym thyng trusted vayne senatours moost part comens inestimable desyre go batayle marius euery man cast mynde inriched prayes spoylynges warre retourne home agayne victours moche honour triumphe thynges otherlyke consydred whiche caused gladly folowe marius also marius dyd nat lytell enbolde confort myndes assembled called togyder great company commen people spake exhortacion confortynge herafter ensueth pthe orison exhortacion consull marius comen people rome voyage numidy whiche exhortacion demonstratyue contaynynge laude prayse marius dysprayse blame noble men rome pthe l chapyter right worthy cytezins knowe well many estate aunciet name haue nat themselfe behaued one maner codicion desyring honorable dignity great office administracion gouernynge haue optayned whyle make peticions begynnyng dyligent seruiable meke curtayse behauoure whan haue optayned desyre passe tyme slouth ydelnes pride semeth mynde ought moche contrarely howe moch valour hole comen wayle cosulshyp thoffice hy iudge great office somoche diligence charge shulde hole comen wele gouerned suche dignity office desyred nat ignorant knowe right well great benefite ye haue gyuen howe great charge besynesse therto belogyng layed vpon withall whiche besynes nedes must sustayne say prepare make redy army withall thynges necessary batayle execute neuertheles spare comen treasour compell warfare batayle suche man wolde nat greue displease comentie rome whome wolde nat displease meanes take charge care euery thyng within cite without thynges among enuious gentylmen obiectyng layeng agaynst euery thynge whiche go men full discorde variance verily noble citezins among suche men take hande suche charge harde thynge dyfficultie man thynke deuyse moreouer cosuls whiche haue ben tyme whan haue done thynge amysse olde noblenesse strong valyant actes predecessor rich power frendes kynsmen many clyentes seruant retayned haue supported mentayned mysdedes richesse helpe trust confort haue selfe nat kynsmen fauourers ayde selfe must necessite defende vertue strenght innocence thynges auncient noble men haue defende vnsure haue nat farthermore noble citezins vnderstande ye haue good trust confidence equall iust good haue fauour vnto knowell good dedes hath profited commen wayle neuerthelesse noble men seke occasion agaynst inuadyng assaylyng malice enuy wherfore standeth hande necessite labour somoche besely quickely neyther ye disceyued great trust whiche ye haue also purpose myne ylwyllers aduersaries may frustrate nothyng auayle agaynst forsoth haue euer chyldhode vnto age ben suche behauour haue ben acustomed exercysed maner labour paryls whiche suffred toke paciently comen wele without rewarde benefite honour whiche ye haue nowe gyuen wherfore worthy citezins seyng yt ye haue rewarded better worthy haue nat purposed desyst leaue myne olde good wyll anenst ye comen wele rewarded purpose nat omyt good dedes dyd frely vnrewarded touchyng aunciet gentylmen hard temper themselfe beyng power dignite onely dyd fayne themselfe good honest optayned promocyon thintent come therby honoure dignite haue passed lyfe right good occupacios cotinuall custome roted well custome tourned nature treuth ye haue comaunded warre agaynst iugurth whiche thynge noble men taketh greuously require consyder dyscus myndes inwarde consideracion ponder ye whyther better necessary expedient change commaundemet agayne sende forth sort auncient gentilmen vnto besynesse agaynst iugurth el lyke send forth noble man olde auncetry honoure remembrance whome many ymages may made erect set vp hy polycie chyualry warfare vtterly ignorant inexpert wyll ye change purpose sende forth suche one warfare pleasure gentylmen sayeth best done cause thintent great mater wighty besynesse suche captayne ignorant ferefull soudyours shalbe chosen whiche anone shal chuse forth agayne one commen people maister informe teche hym suche besynesse office charge belongeth hymselfe beyng ignorant euery thyng necessary done meane often fortuneth whome ye ordayne captayne comaunder army dothe chose captayne commaunder ouer hymselfe somoche ye indifferently iudge whome ye chose capitayne moch mete made symple soudyours capitaynr ouer also worthy citezins knowe noble men farre order whan haue ben made consul haue gyuen themselfe redyng actes elder predecessours grekes preceptes chyualry doutlesse may well called men without order cosyderacion shuld due order first lerne rule office shulde take vpon charge therof contrary first take charge office lerne rule way iordinate howbeit euery wyseman wyll first lerne gouerne office desyre take vpon hym rule therof estate contrarily demeane themselfe thus worthy citezins co pare newe gentylman immoderate pride take diligent considercion whiche best nat gentyll byrth lowly gentyll maners el gentyll blode proude vngentyll maners suche thynges wont rede haue sene selfe haue done haue lerned excercyse chyualrie haue lerned redyng nowe iudge cosyder ye whyther better dedes warkes redynge doyng dispyce neweltie honour vnnoble lynage dispyce vncraftynesse slouth happy fortune obiected agaynst rebuke shame dishonest behauour may obiected layed agaynst rebuke nat trueth euery man come one lyke nature cosyder knowe well one man nat better noble wysdome good maners vertu strength cosyder well euery man endued vertue excellet noble thus strongest wysest moost vertuous moost excellent noblenesse pbut yf father albinus calphurnius la e consul captayns numidy great dishonoure damage empire nowe lyueng myght inquyred whether leuer bene begotten el sayd albinus calphurnius thynke ye wolde answere forsoth nought el suppose wolde desyre couet good chyldren honorable lynage procede stocke generacion thus syth estate dispyseth reasonably ryght lette also dispyce owne predecessours forefather whose stocke lynage proceded came noblenes honour nat auncetry owne strength wysdome vertue lykewyse haue done haue enuy myne honour lette also haue enuy labour taken defence comen wayle let enuy myne innocece great peryls haue ouercoe meanes haue obtayned also shall mentayne honour greatly enuy men corrupt pride ye haue promoted worshyp pa forth tyme yf sette nought office honour optayned vtterly dispised thus desyre dignity duety worthy deserued haue honest lyueng vertuous conuersacion certaynly greatly disceyued whiche loketh two thynges cotrary bothe togyder one season noble men wold haue voluptuous conuersacion progenytours neuer dyscended verely certayne glorious dedes honorable forefather lyke example luminary vnto ofspringe progeny lyght suffreth neyther good dedes bad progeny hyd yf progeny lawfull speke myne owne dedes whiche laude moche clere excellent boost mennes actes nowe cosyder ye vnryghtwyse gentylmen wyll nat graunt laude honoure myne owne vertue actes whiche vsurpe proudely wordes speche shuld abundatly paynted ornate elegant ynough syth cease nat blame reuyle lewde wordes euery place great office ye haue gyuen vnto hath nat pleased styll kepe secrete fautes lest myght count culpable worthy rebuke reason myne indyscrete pacience sylence neuerthelesse sothely wordes nat greue hurt conscyence myne owne mynde say trueth nought say good worshyp wyll nedes ly maners lyuyng couersacion suche shall ouercome wordes proue iniust accusementes fayned false syth counsell blamed noble men bycause ye haue comytted great honoure gretter besynesse cosyder ye myndes diligently often whyther ye shall nede repent dede nat say trueth nat boost selfe ymag genitor nat recout vnto triumphes cosulshyps myne auncetry mater requyred coude well shewe vnto speres standerdes whiche haue taken good worth defence countrey comen wele ymages shewe noblenes nat lefte heritage noblenes haue goten great sore labour body paryll lyfe pmy wordes nat ordred ornate langage spech ypaynted rethorike lyke set lytell therby vertue sheweth selfe playnelie ynough without glosed paynted wordes noble men must necessite haue craft couer shamefull vngoodly dedes eloquent wordes crafty rethorike speche neuer lerned greke letter langage whiche thyng estate obiect agaynst great faut playne pleasure neuer moche lerne thynges haue lytell auayled vnto techers lerner neyther acquisicion vertue expulsion vice haue lerned taught thyng moch better profitable comen wele assayle stryke myne ennemies dispoyle ordynace vitayls chafe garnyson nothing drede feare saue yll name endure take good worth pleasure somer hardenes wynter lyke ly vpon grounde endure hunger labour bothe togyder therfore shall exhort informe soudyours preceptes whiche selfe haue lerned vsed assayed shall nat handell treat theym craft thintent may auaunce richesse vse sharpely selfe plesatly euery difficultie shalbe example labour shall nat put labour take worshyp order profitable thus ought captayne demeane hym among soudyours namely among worthy citezins whan man lyueth delicately hymselfe driueth soudiours peryl batayle punysshemet rygour nat called captayne ruler army rather proude lorde tyrannous oppresser citezins elder worthely behauynge themselfe maner haue made noble excellet inriched comen wele themselfe also estate nowe lyueth trustyng honoured worthynesse genitours theseffe vnlyke codicions despice v haue v disdayne whiche folowe maners genitor euery hye office honour chalange demaunde nat merites duetie heritage othely ouer proude men erre moche trueth though genitor auncetry haue left vnto euery thynge possible leaue rich patrimony ymages remembrace example worthy dedes neuerthelesse vertue haue nat left vnto coude nat kepe onely neyther gyuen vnto rewarde receyued man gentilmen say man without maners vnclenly behauour forsoth bycause prepare dresse nat curyously many delicyous bankettes sufluous deyntyous bycause haue iougler dysar wt moue sportes dissolut laughing curyouse coke one vyllage longyng rural people thyng haue gentylmen haue pleaseth nat knowledge neuer pleasure thynges haue herde father incorrupt well disposed men suche delyciousnesse curyosite belongeth vnto woman labour besynesse belongeth vnto men euery good man thynketh couenient haue plentie worshyp richesse honoure good man haue walles hous garnysshed ouercouered armour wherewith may defend coutrey frendes hymselfe riche ornametes curyous warke profet saue onely syght vayne regarde therof syth gentylmen thus obiect suche mater let cotinue alway vice lyketh haue euer reputed dere let incline voluptuosite daunsyng synging bankettyng playng lechery glotony dronkenes suche vice haue spende youth let pa forth age vtterly subdued bely slepe ydelnes subiect lustes vylest part body let leaue swete fyghting peryll deth blyndyng dust batayle otherlyke paryls vnto v whome acceptable feestes voluptuous bankettes vyle pleasurs nat nat contented vngoodly vyle men haue dishonested themselfe foule dedes redy take way rewardes good men vnto themselfe thus agaynst right lechery slouth moost cursed vyces dothe hurt occupyeth vtter distruction comen wayle comens innocent vnculpable pbut syth haue made answere dysordred gentylmen moderately custome codicion nat largely cursednesse vice ar worthy shall speke nowe fewe thynges touchyng commen wele first al haue ye good trust asperance touchynge besynes numidy ye haue nowe moued auoyded euery thyng wherby iugurth defended begynnynge warre vnto tyme say couetyse calphurnius albinus vncraftynes foly aulus pride metellus founde iugurth socour hytherto auoyded nowe moreouer ye haue army knoweth contrey verily noble manly fortunate happy great part therof wasted spent wors infected corrupted auarice vnboldnesse cowardyse captayns wherfore ye lusty age mete endure hardnesse warre batayle nowe labour ye take ye hande defence commen wayle let none afrayed abasshed misfortune soudyours haue foughten tyme pride captayns myselfe cousellour besynesse felowe peryls shall present euery besynesse bothe iournays batayls also shall gouerne selfe without difference vnder one forme euery poynt verely helpe goddes shall within short season obtayne auatages comodities man may wyn batayle prayes victory immortall laude worshyp certaynlie pleasors auantages dout harde obtayne nat neuerthelesse couenient euery good man ye socour defende co men wayle coutrey fro distruccion dyshonour certaynlie neuer man whiche obtayned immortal laude euerlastynge name cowardise sl uth neuer wyse father wold wysshe chyldren sonnes lyue euer onely myght lyue long behaued themselfe worthely goodnesse honesty passe forth lyfe natural course requireth pworthy romayns wolde speke vnto vnderstode strength coude encreased feble fearfull men wordes nat wherfore semeth haue sayed ynough abundantly noble bolde harted men trust proue phowe marius exhortacion endyd anone laded shyppes ordynance warre sende forwarde one malyus imbassadour howe himselfe anone folowed withal company howe behaued hymselfe numidy fyrste begynnynge pthe li chapyter whan marius vttred ended word vnder forme whan sawe al myndes comens enclined war trust victorie prayes anone without delay caused shyppes charged wt viteyls treasour soudyors wage armour wepyn thynges necessary war comaunded one named aulus manlius assigned embassadours hym departe forwarde shyppes charged meane season marius hymself remayned rome lytel tyme chose forth soudyours suche hym thought expedient nat custome olde romayns predecessours institucion aunciet captayns ordred cartayne maner peple whome soudyours shuld chosen warfare tyme co uenient cotrary wyse marius admytted euery man indifferetly thynge lyckely pleasure go hym many suche admytted also whiche poore nat suffred go warfare lest pouertie myght haue constraned rather fal robbery dedes chiualry beit inacted olde romayns suche excused warre cause aboue sayd gyles suffred nothyng vnprouided vnredy syde syde party ennemies suffred nothyng sure prouided alway preuented uisions pursued often whyle iugurth getulyans spoyled numidyens whiche yelded theselfe whan marius cosydred acre onely glorious excellent without auantage myght nat e ecute batayle iugurth vnstedfastnes mouyng place place consydred mynde ordayned hym redy besyege city countrey one another namely suche outher men place necessary behouable ennemies contrary hurtfull hym dyd thynkynge iugurth without dystourbance suffred hym shuld spoyled bereft city ordynance socours refuge el first bylded hercules whiche borne lande libya nat hercules sonne iupyter alcumena thinhabitours cite ruled iugurth peasably easely put charge besynesse therfore moost true faythful hym defended agaynst al ennemies nat onely walles armour men also moche stronger defence difficultie hardnesse place contrey nere maner impossible army coude coe nere want water scarcite vitels except feldes place myscheuous perilous nature serpentes kyndled ragyng vexed thyrst thyng thyrst coude nat quench want water wherfore neyther man beest myght surely passe wha marius cast al difficulty mynde hert persed company made good prouisyon euery thing might necessary vnto army tyme nede conclusion syxt day whan come sayd flod tana thyder brought myghty multitude bottels bowges made ledder pytched tentes easy bocchus induced hope reward great multitude people came iugurth adioyned army togyder one pat tyme marius copany iournay towarde uince coost affrike apartayned thempire sayd marius purposed rest vnderstandyng comyng ennemies many espyes ouerlate assone worde ennemies euyn hande somoch army coude set order aray coude remoue gather togyder baggage tyme abrode coude take comaundement captayne worde sounde trumpettes horseman maurians getulians ran togyder vpon nat order aray batayle companyes bendes togyder fortuned come togyder heapes cluster romayns moost part al amased greuously fierse syde romayns beat downe ouerthrue wounded mortally many bereft vtterly lyues slewe place remenant sharpely manly resysted compased euery syde aswel behynde assayled neyther manhode strength armour able sufficiently defende maruel ennemies mo nombre compased euery syde finally romayne soudyours bothe olde newe therfore bothe strong bolde crafty batayle gathered nere togyder myght fortuned nombre mete togyder tourned backe backe ioyned rounde one maner compase cercle saued defended themselfe togyder backehalfe man coude assayle yf brake myddes whiche maner impossible maner sustayned myght ennemies also saued themselfe captayne marius ieopardous sharpe besynes nat affrayed al lesse corage boldnesse styred euery batayle men garde hym whome chosen rather strongest boldest men host moost familier hym set audacite tha familiarite namely ieopardous case sotyme socoured soudyours nede sawe paryl somtyme ran amonge ennemies thyckest nat withstandyng resystence assayled valiantly wounded slewe ouerthrue euery syde dyed weapen reed blode blacke mauriens getuliens bycause harde case great troublous noyse rumour coude nat counsel confort soudyours tong therfore thought counsel incorage confort hande gyuyng example surely bestowe stroke many ennemies sende hel cryeng vayne vpon ydo le helpe dartes iauelyns pykes plumettes leed stone suche instrumentes batayle wer cast thicke party ayre therwith indymed stroke coursly charged bright helmes harnesse fyre sprange euery syde semed lyghtnyng cry men dyeng neyeng horse dyn stroke sounde trumpettes horryble tedyous thus continued tyl day lyght passed nyght come numidyans getulians maurians desysted ceassed nothing iugurth bocchus warned comaunded continued sharpely thynking darkenesse nyght shulde auatage marius vnderstadyng toke counsel made best uision hymselfe men whiche myght suche case mater required thintent people myght haue place resort vnto refuge socours prouyded ocupyed two hylles nere togyder whome one ouer narowe lytel groude receyue hole army tentes top therof fayre fountayne pure water moch necessary hyl sufficietly large receyue hole hoost tentes also defensyue great altitude done right euery syde insomoche whiche shulde take hyl sure ynough without great defence themselfe nature sufficiently defended wel considred marius commaunded sylla vndercapten take hym al horsmen tary nyght smaller hyl fountayne done hymselfe gathered togyder lytel lytel remanent soudyours dispersed abrode ennemies nat lesse troubled whan marius thus assembled agayne men togyder led ful cours vp vnto larger hyl thus two kynges iugurth bocchus seyng vayne fyght whiche hyer groude also sure place costrayned leaue fyght difficultie place romayns taken neuertheles meane tyme suffred nat men depart far then compased bothe hylles roud hole multitude taryed rested shed abrode vpon ground whan taken place maner made great fiers many place hoost barbarian custome passed forth part night myrth pleasure gladnes reioysing daunsyng making great noyse dyn rennyng goyng place place loudly crieng synging reuellyng kynges themselfe also nat lytel proude fearse bycause nat fled batayle counted themselfe ouercomers seyng helde romayns besieged thought durst nat abyde part romais intetyfly gaue aduertes demeanour ennemies romayns hyght hyl without lyght therfore easy darknesse hyer place parceyued al dedes behauour ennemies beneth moch euidently light fyers vnwyse behauour numidiens put romayns great confort great courage specially marius greatly confermed hope seyng negligence folly vncraftinesse wherfore comaunded folke kepe sylence styl might possible without noyse somoche suffred nat trupetes soude watche warryours ar wont agaynst night afterwarde whan day began apere numidiens al weryed wt cryeng ouerlate watchyng reuel gyuen theselfe rest lytel men without feare dout ye romayns certenly true uerbe often sayd fayre wether succedeth tepestious cloudes aft myrth ioye often cometh sadnes sorowe hapened numidyes whyle ingorged fylled wynes lay slepyng grounde beestes without fere without uision marius comauded sodenly trumpetes clarionistes mynstrels sound instrumetes shyrle coude altogyder al soudyours shulde set vp shout cry horribly myght inuade breke tentes numidyens shortly done wherfore numidyens mauriens getuliens astonyed abasshed vnknowen horryble noyse sodenly awakened sleape seyng thus copased ennemies feare deth noyse amased power neyther fle drawe armour vtterly prouid maner socour themselfe thus stode astonyed horrible noyse cry yf madnesshe entred none able socour hymselfe romayns alway increased noyse feare assayling murdring woundyng without resystence finally al outher ouerthrowen slayne wouded el fled armor standerdes weapen left behynde mo batayle slayne al batels amonge al none taken prisoner fere sleape amased fewe escaped flight pof great prouysion wysdome marius victory seconde batayle agaynst two kynges also great vyctory laude honour pthe lvii chapyter whan marius gloriously thus ouer come moost part ennemies except two kyng drue hym towarde wyntring place purposed ordred hymselfe men specially hauen townes bycause easy uision vytels neuertheles iournay thyderwarde al victory becam nat negligent vnware proude captayns often ar wont aft victory goten ennemies uided went forwarde army quadrat deuided four partes ordred apoynted ennemies ben sight sylla assigned take charge ryght wyng army al spear men hym aulus manlius lyft wyng hym slyngars archer cohortes lumbardes peticapitayns fotemen lyght harnesse distributed dyuided vantgarde rerewarde treatours whiche forsaken iugurth came romayns suche best laboured knewe best contrey chosen forth sent espy contrey wayes iugurth bocchus nat withstandyng marius hymselfe prouident circuspect diligent withal comytted charge none mouyng cotinually place place ouer army laudyng comendyng rewardyng good soudyors blamyng rebukyng bad hym selfe armed diligently prouidyng ministryng vnto euery thyng necessary expedient copelled frowarde ylwillyng labour euery place set tentes iournay ordred defence depe dyches trench rounde hoost entres tentes assigned soudyors elect therto kepe watch kepe scoutwatch tentes compasse moreouer ordred castynge dyches outwarde bulwarkes defende remanent sodayne peryl apered hymselfe armed nyghtly wet serched watch nat specially feare mystrust paryl come feare soudyours wold nat obey comaundemet specially thentent loudyours seyng captayne nat refusyng labour paryl shuld also wylling folowe take payne vpon themselfe ashamed dyd nat asmoch captayn certenly tyme many warre rede marius costrayned soudyors labour rather shame tha wt sharpnes punisshemet shame seruant ydle wha maister sore laboreth howbeit sayd marius toke labour vpon hym desyre comendacion worshyp bycause fro youth euer wont hardnesse hunger thirst labour many thynges whiche delycate gentylmen tyme count misery marius hardness moche pleasure delyte affection whiche agaynst commen wayle equal persones supposed euer intent marius treated army wyse knowen dedes dyd asmoche profet worshyp commen wayle rome rigorously sharpely treated soudyours al thynges ordred wel worthely honour profet commen wayle rigorously treated army pbut retourne purpose whan marius suche dyligence sayd come nat far towne cirtha last fourth day forsayd batayle espyes ennemies appered euery syde romais vnderstode anone therby ennemies hande espyes romains also sende forth brought tidynges euery coost coutrey marius perceyued ennemies diuerse copanyes deuided wherfore vncertayne howe myght best order hoost receyue therfore perceyuing vnsure order forfront batayle ought abode ennemies place order chaunged hoost deuyded iiii partes sayd whiche redy prouyded euery chauce thus iugurth disceyued frustrate purpose deuyded hoost four partes trustynge inuade romayns backehalfe parte army part encouter two partes enclose sydes enuyron rounde mean tyme sylla first encountred iugurth exhorted coforted men aswel might breuite tyme done anone proceded company bendes clustres togyder horse conioyned moost thyckest maner fiersly assayled maurians remanent fotemen whiche vnder sylla remayned kept themselfe styl first place defended bodyes dartes whiche ennemies thrue agaynst farre chaunsed ennemies come bytwene handes hewed downe decrease nombre pwhyle sylla horsmen thus fiersly fightyng right wyng batayle kyng bocchus assembled togyder fotemen whome son named volux brought thyder hym fotemen suche impediment iournay thyderwarde came ouerlate batayle whiche last foughten wherfore bocchus whan assembled inbolded word fresshe fotemen assayled fiersly rerewarde romayns pin meane tyme marius hymself occupyed forwarde hoost employed wysdome strength valyant worthy captayne stode hym hande forwarde iugurth hymselfe grettest power strogest copany men inbatayled hym pbut iugurth knewe comyng bocchus felde anone turned hym smal copany hym priuely vnto fotemen romayns hye voyse cried vnto sayng fought vayne lytel slayne marius owne handes cryeng wordes lyfted vp withal shewed swerde al ouersprincled dyed blode whiche couloured batayle fiersly ynough murdring fotemen romayns wordes iugurth cryed latyn tong lerned speke latyn longe batayle numaunce whan romayns herde wordes affrayed crueltie noyse confidence trust whiche messanger ye syde myndes barbariens wer bolded exalted wordes reason wherof sharpely inuaded romayns seynge abasshed astonyed nowe romains forwarde poynt redy gyue themselfe flyght men dyscouraged sayd tidynges pwhan poynt fortuned tyme sylla beaten ouerthrowen mauriens inuaded assayled hym right wyng batayle wherfore retourned copany fiersly assayled fresshe fotemen wer bocchus one syde brake amonge thyckest bocchus anone tourned backe gaue hymselfe flyght pon othersyde iugurth part batayle almost optayned vyctory dyd diligence incourage support copany mentayne auatage whiche coclusion al vayne whyle laboured worthy captayne spear men romayns copased hym copany ye right syde lyft al garde hym conclusion slayne hymselfe glad saue lyfe brake forth alone among ye myddes ennemies wepyns dartes great difficuly pbut meane tyme marius ouercome driuen away horsmen assayled hym wherfore anone returned fiersly helpe socours company whome vnderstode somwhat put backe violece ennemies policy valiant dedes anone reconforted men none ennemies able withstande violence part batayle pthus finally romayns great labour many greuous woundes disconfited ennemies euery syde whan batayle ended romayns began pursue chase verily pytefull horrible syght beholde open feldes consyder cruel spectacle batayle howe fled pursued inraged murdring rored dyeng slayne taken prisoner horse men mengled togyder labouring panges deth ground ouerspred deed corps mangled mutulate horribly hewyn inuolued blode cogeled horse wounded mad drewe deed carcase maisters legges hangyng styropes grounde somtyme laboured ryse auoyde anone feblenes fel downe ground agayne eche rowlyng turnyng blode finally far mannes syght myght extende al grounde ouerspred couered armour wepen deed caryons rennyng blode al ground infect horryble beholde phowe bocchus thus twyse ouercom batel purposed make peace romains howe request marius sende vnto hym sylla manlius knowe mynde behalfe pthe lviii chapiter batel thus ended vtter damage distruction numidyans laude honour romayns marius nowe without dout ouercomer victour went vnto towne cirtha iournay purpose first begynnyng two batayls whan marius soiourned fyue dayes aft batayle came vnto hym embassador fro kyng bocchus whiche kyng behalfe desyred marius sende vnto hym two trusty men whiche sayng wold comen treate dyuers besynesses owne profet fet auatage romains also marius without tary sende forth sylla one aulus manlius whan come kyng bocchus howbeit sende comen mater neuertheles cocluded bytwene speke hym first thentent kyndell inflame mynde agaynst iugurth el seyng hym somwhat desyrous wyllyng haue peace prouoke hym wt desyre therto wherfore sylla manlius gaue place nat age bur eloquence began spake bocchus maner foloweth pof wordes sylla tresourer romayne army kyng bocch lix cha king bocchus haue great gladnes ioye syth goddes haue thus admonisshed enspired noble man last ye haue reputed peace better acceptable war lest ye myght dishonest defyle worthynesse associating yourselfe moost vnhappy tyran iugurth also ar glad ye haue auoyded occasion necessite wherby moued pursue batayle beyng ignorant quarel copany ye sayd cursed iugurth tyran ennemy thempyre rome certenly ye people rome euer syth poore simple smal begynning haue thought better wyn fredes seruates bondman also haue thought moch surer thyng haue vnder empire suche wyllingly owne mocion wolde yelde theselfe haue costrayned therto agaynst wyl verily frendshyp necessary amyte frendshyp first al bycause ye farre sonder wherby shal haue le power greue put charge reason frendshyp fauour thankes may redy nere togyder cosydering many great frendes whiche haue nat far march also vnto thempire rome obeyers subgettes seruantes abundantly touchyng louers frendes none haue sufficiently ynough consideracion kynge bocchus fredshyp shalbe acceptable vnto v wolde god pleased thus haue done begynning war forsoth ye done shulde ye tyme haue receyued romayns mo comodites auantages good dedes ye haue nowe suffred losse damage hurtes whyle mannes dedes besynesses moost part ruled fortune whiche fortune hath pleased ye shuld proue assay myght violence batayle also loue fauour peace therfore nowe syht amytie proferred suffraunce fortune syth lauful take nat slowe hen forwarde hastely procede ye haue begon ye may proue romayns frendes lyke ye haue proued ennemies tyme ye haue many expedient oportunites necessary comodites whome ye may make amendes wt good dedes ye haue offe ded agaynst romayns ouerpasse olde fautes newe kyndnesses benefites finally fix hert ye shal neuer ouercome peple rome kyndnes good dedes touchynge hatered myght ar batayle yet yourselfe knowe profe experience wherfore procede acquiring frendshyp whiche gladly shalbe graunted vnto merites shal deserue pof answere bocchus made sylla vnstablenesse mynde bocchus pthe lx chapyter wordes sylla answered bocchus myldely soberly fewe wordes spake excusing offence done agayne romayns sayeng nat taken armour begon war agaynst ennemy iniury wrong vnto defende owne kyngdome thirde part numidy belonged vnto hym lawe armes romayns laboured expel iugurth doyng distroyed part contrey whiche coude nat suffer vnreuenged moreouer bocchus sayd hymselfe sende vnto rome require amyte frendshyp romayns thing vnto hym denyed coclusion sayd wolde omyt lay part al olde malyce althyng shulde done agreed bytwene yf marius wolde graut hym embassadours might sende rome sayd frendship cofederate ye romains vpon answere sylla felawe retourned marius whiche anone agreed yt embassador shuld set rome shortly tyme iugurth vnderstode comyng sylla manlius feared thyng whiche ordend hande anone wt rewardes corrupted frendes bocchus agayn chauged mynde counsel mutable variable mynde phow bocchus changed purpose yet one agayne sende newe embassadours marius treat peace howe sylla receyued treated absence marius pthe lxi chapyter meane tyme marius set ordred hoost wyntring place toke wt hym men lyght harnesse also part horseman went desart nat far then besige certayne towre belongyng iugurth whiche towre sayd iugurth put garnyson defence al treators forsaken fled romayns iugurth mean whyle bocchus new agayne cosydred mynde misfortune whiche hapened hym two batayls el counsel frendes whome iugurth nat corrupted reward chose forth among al v men whose fidelite trueth wel knowen often proued whose wysdome expert redy sende marius comauded afterwarde mater required embassador take way rome comitted ful authorite euery thyng done coclude war euer maner shuld seme best moost expediet discrecion embassadours toke le e spedely toke iournay place romayns soiourned wynter season whyle wer iournay thyderwarde assayled theues getulians robbed spoyled al thus last without worshyp apparel affrayed abasshed fled vnto sylla refuge sylla left marius wynteryng place ruler romayne army absence tyme embassador thus spoyled come sylla refuge receyued nat fayntly vayne vnstable ennemies deserued curteysly moch gentylnes liberalite treatynge al poyntes honorably meanes barbarias rude people counted supposed name couetyse whiche imputed vnto romayns comen fame false fayned ennemies distayne honour also moch liberalite sylla counted hym special frende yet vnto tyme accloyeng gyftes gyuen rewardes policy falshode ouercoe couetous simple myndes vnknowen vnto many man liberal gyft thought couted faythful hert withal thus barbarian reputed liberte reward sylla great euident token loue demed purpose embassadours anone opened declared nat owne sekyng cursed faut prouocacion instygation iugurth wherof kynge sore repented wherfore behalfe conclusyon besought romayns pardon amyte peace brefely answered maner pthe senatours people rome whan shal deserue phow marius sent sylla agayne bocchus desyre danger sylla escaped helpe volux son kyng bocchus pthe lxiii chapyter whan bocchus vnderstode al thinges desyred marius letter sende vnto iournay sodenly volux son bocchus apered shewed hymselfe romayns open feldes mo men went scatered dyspersed abrode neglygetly semed sylla al greatter nombre dede sylla al company feared thinkynge ennemies wherfore romayns made redy armour weapen defende themselfe resyst ennemies nede shulde requyre lytel feare amonge hope confort ouerpassed feare vpper hande consydred shulde bycker whome often ouerthrowen ouercome meane tyme horseman whiche sent party espy ye trueth mater certified eche al thyng quyet sure ynough dede without treason paryl volux metyng called sylla name welcomed hym benyngely sayeng sent father bocchus mete sayd sylla honour socour defence proceded forthewarde al day next day company togyder without feare daunger nyght tentes pytched sodenly maurian volux came rennyng sylla al pale quakyng sayd infourmed espyes iugurth nat far then prayed exhorted hym fle away wt hym priuely nyght sylla denyed vtterly fierse bolde courage sayeng feared nat cowarde numidyan often ben ouercome trusted wel ynough strength courage men finally gaue volux answere knewe without dout sure distruction instat myne shuld slayne felde yet wold nat fle drede rather abyde dye manfully cowardely flee shame people whome haue charge sparyng lyues whiche incertayne vnsure parauenture shortly shal fynisshe sickenes dysease nat better dye noble quarel manly tha lyue shame cowardly whan sylla thus answered volux couselled hym depart place remoue forward nyght therto sylla cosented anone comaunded soudyours refresshe tentes vitels make plenty fiers ouer al place intent yf ennemies nere beholdyng fiers shulde thynke wolde nat remoue then nyght first hour night sylla comaunded al soudyors leaue fiers brennynge depart forwarde iournay scilence dyd went al night long euyn sonne rysinge al beyng weryed sylla pytched tentes agayne certayne horseman mauriens brought word iugurth taken place tentes rested distance two myle whan tidynges harde among romayns meruelous great fear entred myndes al thought themselfe betrayed volux enuyrounde falshode treason many aduysed take punisshemet volux sayeng thyng vnworthy suffre hym escape vnpunysshed great myschefe treason agaynst commytted howbeit sylla inwardly opynion neuertheles defended maurian dammage exhorted men strong bolde myndes sayeng often tyme ben sene fewe worthy men victory moche multitude coward howe moch lesse spared bodyes batayle fro fightyng somoch surer shuld semed man whome god nature gyuen handes defende body sicke defence fete vnarmed rennyng away suche ieopardy noble soudyour ought nat tourne away body ennemy though naked vnarmed pwhan sylla exhorted men suche wordes called vnto hym volux called wytnesse iupyter al ydols recorde falshode treason bocchus father volux betrayed hym asmoch sylla supposed volux brought hym treason handes iugurth counsel comaundement father bocchus comaunded volux anone depart copany syght volux pytuously wepyng besought sylla nat byleue suche thing hym sayd certenly gyle treason nothyng done father rather iugurth subtilte espyed serched iournay wayes espies knowen coclusion said volux syth iugurth hath great copany hope trust confort ye moost part dependeth father thinke shal nat bolde damage openly whyle copany may recorde ded father wherfore sylla thentent ye may parceyue treason shal openly go alone ye myddes tentes iugurth sauely conuey sede folke el leaue hexe company whyther shal please best cousel alowed sylla anone without tary proceded forwarde al co pany myddes tentes iugurth bycause sodenly done iugurth nat knowyng subtylte espy cousel assone hard bocchus sende sylla numidyan moch familierly couersat bocchus tyme moreouer named dabar son massagrade father syde stocke massinissa mother syde vnlyke byrth mother borne cocubine dabar haue sayd season also copany bocchus hym dere welbeloued subtel wyt great actes whiche done namely bycause bocchus founde proued hym trusty faythful many tymes anone bocchus sende dabar sylla commaundyng dabar shewe hym yt redy euery thyng ye romains hym wolde comaunde assigne sylla hymself shuld apoynt chose tyme place might comen togyder mater shulde nat fere dout though embassadoure iugurth hym reserued thyng touchyng cousel hole tyll comyng sylla nothyng apoynted comuned cocluded imbassadour iugurth imbassadour called thyder thyntent comen besynesses might done
